   214                                           @profile
   215                                           def iterativePrunning(i, m, cH, description, biomassRxn, lb_biomass,
   216                                                                 repetition, thresh = 1E-10, EXrxns = [],
   217                                                                 EXtrrxns = [], Othertrrxns = []):
   218                                               """
   219                                               solver can be 'cplex', 'glpk' or 'gurobi'
   220                                               """
   221         1            1      1.0      0.0      if len(EXrxns) > 0:
   222                                                   EXrxnsprune = list(set(list(EXrxns)) - cH)
   223                                                   random.shuffle(EXrxnsprune)
   224                                                   while EXrxnsprune:
   225                                                       rxn1 = EXrxnsprune.pop()
   226                                                       try:
   227                                                           mTemp1 = pruneRxn(mTemp1, cH, rxn1, thresh, description,
   228                                                                             repetition, biomassRxn, lb_biomass)
   229                                                           EXrxnsprune2 = []
   230                                                           for k in mTemp1.idRs:
   231                                                               if k in EXrxnsprune:
   232                                                                   EXrxnsprune2.append(k)
   233                                                           random.shuffle(EXrxnsprune2)
   234                                                           EXrxnsprune = EXrxnsprune2
   235                                                       except NameError:
   236                                                           mTemp1 = pruneRxn(m, cH, rxn1, thresh, description,
   237                                                                             repetition, biomassRxn, lb_biomass)
   238                                                           EXrxnsprune2 = []
   239                                                           for k in mTemp1.idRs:
   240                                                               if k in EXrxnsprune:
   241                                                                   EXrxnsprune2.append(k)
   242                                                           random.shuffle(EXrxnsprune2)
   243                                                           EXrxnsprune = EXrxnsprune2
   244         1            1      1.0      0.0      if len(EXtrrxns) > 0:
